 Usually when people go to withdraw money from the ATM, they get as much cash as they want to withdraw
 lekin bihar ke jahanabad main ek atm aisa bhi he jahaan vyakti jitne paise nikaalnaa chahta he to ATM uskaa 20 guna use detaa he
 It must have been strange to hear this, but it is true
 isiilie kaha ja rahaa he ki jahanabad kaa yah ATM dhanavarsha karata he
 In fact, on Friday evening money started raining from the ATM of Indian Bank near Jehanabad railway station
 graahak ke 100 rupee nikaalane par ATM use 2000 nikalakar de rahaa tha, yani 20 guna zyada
 The talk of Dhan Varshan of the ATM of Jehanabad spread like fire in the city and in a short time people withdrew 8 lakh 72 thousand from this bank
 jab isalaathn se dhanavarsha kii baat indian bank ke aalaa adhikariyon ko pataa chali to unke hosh ud gaye or aanan-fanan main unhone is ATM par taala jad diya
 Regarding the entire matter, the branch manager of Indian Bank Abhishek Kumar said that there was some mistake from the engineer while servicing the ATM, due to which ₹ 2000 was being withdrawn instead of ₹ 100
 kumaar ne bataaya ki ATM main note rakhane ke liye 3 casette hote hai jisamen sabase upar 2000 kaa note hota he, uske neeche 500 or sabase neeche 100 kaa note hota he
 During the last servicing, the engineer had accidentally placed the cassette giving ₹ 2000 at the bottom
 jisaki vajah se jab bhi koi vyakti 100 rupee nikaal rahaa tha to use 2000 kaa note mil rahaa tha
 Due to this mistake, the branch manager told that the people of 8 lakh 72 thousand rupees will be withdrawn, that they will try their best to get the money back in some way
